1. Role Type Definition (Identity Layer)\\n\\nThe fundamental role types are defined in `pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go` with constants RoleViewer, RoleEditor, and RoleAdmin. These are re-exported in `pkg/services/org/model.go` for organization-level management.\\n\\n## 2. Role-to-Permission Mapping\\n\\n**Core Definitions:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go`: Contains `DeclareFixedRoles()` function that registers fixed role definitions and `BasicRolePrefix` constant ('basic:') for role naming\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/models.go`: Defines the `Permission` struct and provides `PermissionsForActions()` and `ConcatPermissions()` utility functions for creating permission sets\\n\\n**Role Registration:**\\nThe `DeclareFixedRoles()` function in roles.go registers three basic roles:\\n- `basic_viewer`: View-only permissions (folders:read, dashboards:read, etc.)\\n- `basic_editor`: Edit permissions (folders:write, dashboards:write, etc.)\\n- `basic_admin`: Admin permissions (folders.permissions:write, dashboards.permissions:write, etc.)\\n\\n## 3. Permission Guard Middleware\\n\\n**Middleware Stack:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go`: Implements the `Middleware()` function that wraps HTTP handlers with permission checking. It evaluates permissions using the AccessControl interface.\\n- `pkg/middleware/auth.go`: Contains higher-level authentication and authorization middleware including role-based protection\\n\\n**Permission Evaluation:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/evaluator.go`: Defines the `Evaluator` interface and implements permission checking logic:\\n  - `EvalPermission()`: Creates an evaluator for a specific action and scope\\n  - `EvalAll()`: Requires all conditions to pass (AND logic)\\n  - `EvalAny()`: Requires at least one condition to pass (OR logic)\\n  - `Evaluate()`: Method that checks if a user's permissions satisfy the evaluator\\n\\n**Core Authorization:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/accesscontrol.go`: Implements the `AccessControl` interface with `Evaluate()` and `HasAccess()` functions that orchestrate permission checking\\n- `pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go`: Implements RBAC authorization with `checkPermission()` and `checkInheritedPermissions()` methods for detailed permission evaluation\\n\\n## 4. Folder and Dashboard Permission Inheritance\\n\\n**Folder Permissions:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go`: Implements `FolderPermissionsService` via `ProvideFolderPermissions()`, defines folder-specific actions (ActionFoldersRead, ActionFoldersWrite, ActionFoldersPermissionsWrite)\\n- `pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder.go`: Folder service implementation with permission enforcement on create/read/update/delete operations\\n- `pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder_unifiedstorage.go`: Unified storage implementation handling folder permissions\\n\\n**Dashboard Permissions:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go`: Implements `DashboardPermissionsService` via `ProvideDashboardPermissions()`, defines dashboard-specific actions\\n- `pkg/services/dashboards/models.go`: Dashboard and folder model definitions\\n\\n**Inherited Scopes (Permission Inheritance):**\\n- `pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go`: Implements `GetInheritedScopes()` function that traverses the folder hierarchy and returns all parent folder scopes for a dashboard, enabling permission inheritance from folders to dashboards\\n- `pkg/services/searchV2/auth.go`: Uses inherited scopes to filter search results based on hierarchical permissions\\n- `pkg/services/sqlstore/permissions/dashboard.go`: Database layer that implements permission filtering for dashboards considering folder inheritance\\n\\n**Permission Types:**\\n- `pkg/services/dashboards/dashboardaccess/dashboard_access.go`: Defines legacy permission types:\\n  - `PERMISSION_VIEW` (1)\\n  - `PERMISSION_EDIT` (2)\\n  - `PERMISSION_ADMIN` (4)\\n\\n## 5.
